67// SX127x common LoRa modem settings
68// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OP_MODE MSB LSB DESCRIPTION
69#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FSK_OOK 0b00000000 // 7 7 FSK/OOK mode
70#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LORA 0b10000000 // 7 7 LoRa mode
71#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_ACCESS_SHARED_REG_OFF 0b00000000 // 6 6 access LoRa registers (0x0D:0x3F) in LoRa mode
72#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_ACCESS_SHARED_REG_ON 0b01000000 // 6 6 access FSK registers (0x0D:0x3F) in LoRa mode
73#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SLEEP 0b00000000 // 2 0 sleep
74#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_STANDBY 0b00000001 // 2 0 standby
75#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FSTX 0b00000010 // 2 0 frequency synthesis TX
76#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_TX 0b00000011 // 2 0 transmit
77#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FSRX 0b00000100 // 2 0 frequency synthesis RX
78#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RXCONTINUOUS 0b00000101 // 2 0 receive continuous
79#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RXSINGLE 0b00000110 // 2 0 receive single
80#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CAD 0b00000111 // 2 0 channel activity detection
81
82// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_PA_CONFIG
83#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PA_SELECT_RFO 0b00000000 // 7 7 RFO pin output, power limited to +14 dBm
84#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PA_SELECT_BOOST 0b10000000 // 7 7 PA_BOOST pin output, power limited to +20 dBm
85#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OUTPUT_POWER 0b00001111 // 3 0 output power: P_out = 2 + OUTPUT_POWER [dBm] for PA_SELECT_BOOST
86 // P_out = -1 + OUTPUT_POWER [dBm] for PA_SELECT_RFO
87
88// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OCP
89#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OCP_OFF 0b00000000 // 5 5 PA overload current protection disabled
90#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OCP_ON 0b00100000 // 5 5 PA overload current protection enabled
91#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OCP_TRIM 0b00001011 // 4 0 OCP current: I_max(OCP_TRIM = 0b1011) = 100 mA
92
93// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_LNA
94#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_1 0b00100000 // 7 5 LNA gain setting: max gain
95#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_2 0b01000000 // 7 5 .
96#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_3 0b01100000 // 7 5 .
97#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_4 0b10000000 // 7 5 .
98#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_5 0b10100000 // 7 5 .
99#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_GAIN_6 0b11000000 // 7 5 min gain
100#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_BOOST_OFF 0b00000000 // 1 0 default LNA current
101#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_LNA_BOOST_ON 0b00000011 // 1 0 150% LNA current
102
103// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_MODEM_CONFIG_2
104#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_6 0b01100000 // 7 4 spreading factor: 64 chips/bit
105#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_7 0b01110000 // 7 4 128 chips/bit
106#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_8 0b10000000 // 7 4 256 chips/bit
107#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_9 0b10010000 // 7 4 512 chips/bit
108#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_10 0b10100000 // 7 4 1024 chips/bit
109#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_11 0b10110000 // 7 4 2048 chips/bit
110#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SF_12 0b11000000 // 7 4 4096 chips/bit
111#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_TX_MODE_SINGLE 0b00000000 // 3 3 single TX
112#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_TX_MODE_CONT 0b00001000 // 3 3 continuous TX
113#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TIMEOUT_MSB 0b00000000 // 1 0
114
115// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_SYMB_TIMEOUT_LSB
116#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TIMEOUT_LSB 0b01100100 // 7 0 10-bit RX operation timeout
117
118// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_PREAMBLE_MSB + REG_PREAMBLE_LSB
119#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PREAMBLE_LENGTH_MSB 0b00000000 // 7 0 2-byte preamble length setting: l_P = PREAMBLE_LENGTH + 4.25
120#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PREAMBLE_LENGTH_LSB 0b00001000 // 7 0 where l_p = preamble length
121
122// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_DETECT_OPTIMIZE
123#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DETECT_OPTIMIZE_SF_6 0b00000101 // 2 0 SF6 detection optimization
124#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DETECT_OPTIMIZE_SF_7_12 0b00000011 // 2 0 SF7 to SF12 detection optimization
125
126// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_INVERT_IQ
127#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_INVERT_IQ_RXPATH_ON 0b01000000 // 6 6 I and Q signals are inverted
128#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_INVERT_IQ_RXPATH_OFF 0b00000000 // 6 6 normal mode
129#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_INVERT_IQ_TXPATH_ON 0b00000001 // 0 0 I and Q signals are inverted
130#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_INVERT_IQ_TXPATH_OFF 0b00000000 // 0 0 normal mode
131
132// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_DETECTION_THRESHOLD
133#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DETECTION_THRESHOLD_SF_6 0b00001100 // 7 0 SF6 detection threshold
134#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DETECTION_THRESHOLD_SF_7_12 0b00001010 // 7 0 SF7 to SF12 detection threshold
135
136// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_PA_DAC
137#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PA_BOOST_OFF 0b00000100 // 2 0 PA_BOOST disabled
138#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PA_BOOST_ON 0b00000111 // 2 0 +20 dBm on PA_BOOST when OUTPUT_POWER = 0b1111
139
140// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_HOP_PERIOD
141#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_HOP_PERIOD_OFF 0b00000000 // 7 0 number of periods between frequency hops; 0 = disabled
142#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_HOP_PERIOD_MAX 0b11111111 // 7 0

144// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_IRQ_FLAGS
145#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_RX_TIMEOUT 0b10000000 // 7 7 timeout
146#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_RX_DONE 0b01000000 // 6 6 packet reception complete
147#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_PAYLOAD_CRC_ERROR 0b00100000 // 5 5 payload CRC error
148#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_VALID_HEADER 0b00010000 // 4 4 valid header received
149#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_TX_DONE 0b00001000 // 3 3 payload transmission complete
150#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_CAD_DONE 0b00000100 // 2 2 CAD complete
151#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_FHSS_CHANGE_CHANNEL 0b00000010 // 1 1 FHSS change channel
152#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_CLEAR_IRQ_FLAG_CAD_DETECTED 0b00000001 // 0 0 valid LoRa signal detected during CAD operation
153
154// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_IRQ_FLAGS_MASK
155#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_RX_TIMEOUT 0b01111111 // 7 7 timeout
156#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_RX_DONE 0b10111111 // 6 6 packet reception complete
157#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_PAYLOAD_CRC_ERROR 0b11011111 // 5 5 payload CRC error
158#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_VALID_HEADER 0b11101111 // 4 4 valid header received
159#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_TX_DONE 0b11110111 // 3 3 payload transmission complete
160#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_CAD_DONE 0b11111011 // 2 2 CAD complete
161#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_FHSS_CHANGE_CHANNEL 0b11111101 // 1 1 FHSS change channel
162#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MASK_IRQ_FLAG_CAD_DETECTED 0b11111110 // 0 0 valid LoRa signal detected during CAD operation
163

172#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_SYNC_WORD_LORAWAN 0x34 // 7 0 sync word reserved for LoRaWAN networks

233// SX127x common FSK modem settings
234// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OP_MODE
235#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MODULATION_FSK 0b00000000 // 6 5 FSK modulation scheme
236#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_MODULATION_OOK 0b00100000 // 6 5 OOK modulation scheme
237#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX 0b00000101 // 2 0 receiver mode
238
239// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_BITRATE_MSB + SX127X_REG_BITRATE_LSB
240#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_BITRATE_MSB 0x1A // 7 0 bit rate setting: BitRate = F(XOSC)/(BITRATE + BITRATE_FRAC/16)
241#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_BITRATE_LSB 0x0B // 7 0 default value: 4.8 kbps
242
243// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_FDEV_MSB + SX127X_REG_FDEV_LSB
244#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FDEV_MSB 0x00 // 5 0 frequency deviation: Fdev = Fstep * FDEV
245#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FDEV_LSB 0x52 // 7 0 default value: 5 kHz
246
247// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_RX_CONFIG
248#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RESTART_RX_ON_COLLISION_OFF 0b00000000 // 7 7 automatic receiver restart disabled (default)
249#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RESTART_RX_ON_COLLISION_ON 0b10000000 // 7 7 automatically restart receiver if it gets saturated or on packet collision
250#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RESTART_RX_WITHOUT_PLL_LOCK 0b01000000 // 6 6 manually restart receiver without frequency change
251#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RESTART_RX_WITH_PLL_LOCK 0b00100000 // 5 5 manually restart receiver with frequency change
252#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_AFC_AUTO_OFF 0b00000000 // 4 4 no AFC performed (default)
253#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_AFC_AUTO_ON 0b00010000 // 4 4 AFC performed at each receiver startup
254#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_AGC_AUTO_OFF 0b00000000 // 3 3 LNA gain set manually by register
255#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_AGC_AUTO_ON 0b00001000 // 3 3 LNA gain controlled by AGC
256#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_NONE 0b00000000 // 2 0 receiver startup at: none
257#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_RSSI_INTERRUPT 0b00000001 // 2 0 RSSI interrupt
258#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_PREAMBLE_DETECT 0b00000110 // 2 0 preamble detected
259#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_BOTH 0b00000111 // 2 0 RSSI interrupt and preamble detected
260
261// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_RSSI_CONFIG
262#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_2 0b00000000 // 2 0 number of samples for RSSI average: 2
263#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_4 0b00000001 // 2 0 4
264#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_8 0b00000010 // 2 0 8 (default)
265#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_16 0b00000011 // 2 0 16
266#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_32 0b00000100 // 2 0 32
267#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_64 0b00000101 // 2 0 64
268#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_128 0b00000110 // 2 0 128
269#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_SMOOTHING_SAMPLES_256 0b00000111 // 2 0 256
270
271// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_RSSI_COLLISION
272#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_COLLISION_THRESHOLD 0x0A // 7 0 RSSI threshold in dB that will be considered a collision, default value: 10 dB
273
274// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_RSSI_THRESH
275#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RSSI_THRESHOLD 0xFF // 7 0 RSSI threshold that will trigger RSSI interrupt, RssiThreshold = RSSI_THRESHOLD / 2 [dBm]
276
277// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_RX_BW
278#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_MANT_16 0b00000000 // 4 3 channel filter bandwidth: RxBw = F(XOSC) / (RxBwMant * 2^(RxBwExp + 2)) [kHz]
279#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_MANT_20 0b00001000 // 4 3
280#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_MANT_24 0b00010000 // 4 3 default RxBwMant parameter
281#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_EXP 0b00000101 // 2 0 default RxBwExp parameter
282
283// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_AFC_BW
284#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_MANT_AFC 0b00001000 // 4 3 default RxBwMant parameter used during AFC
285#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_RX_BW_EXP_AFC 0b00000011 // 2 0 default RxBwExp parameter used during AFC
286
287// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OOK_PEAK
288#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_BIT_SYNC_OFF 0b00000000 // 5 5 bit synchronizer disabled (not allowed in packet mode)
289#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_BIT_SYNC_ON 0b00100000 // 5 5 bit synchronizer enabled (default)
290#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_THRESH_FIXED 0b00000000 // 4 3 OOK threshold type: fixed value
291#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_THRESH_PEAK 0b00001000 // 4 3 peak mode (default)
292#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_THRESH_AVERAGE 0b00010000 // 4 3 average mode
293#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_0_5_DB 0b00000000 // 2 0 OOK demodulator step size: 0.5 dB (default)
294#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_1_0_DB 0b00000001 // 2 0 1.0 dB
295#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_1_5_DB 0b00000010 // 2 0 1.5 dB
296#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_2_0_DB 0b00000011 // 2 0 2.0 dB
297#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_3_0_DB 0b00000100 // 2 0 3.0 dB
298#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_4_0_DB 0b00000101 // 2 0 4.0 dB
299#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_5_0_DB 0b00000110 // 2 0 5.0 dB
300#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_6_0_DB 0b00000111 // 2 0 6.0 dB
301
302// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OOK_FIX
303#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_FIXED_THRESHOLD 0x0C // 7 0 default fixed threshold for OOK data slicer

305// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OOK_AVG

559#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DIO5_PACK_DATA 0b00100000 // 5 4
560#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DIO5_PACK_MODE_READY 0b00110000 // 5 4
561#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DIO_MAP_PREAMBLE_DETECT 0b00000001 // 0 0
562#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_DIO_MAP_RSSI 0b00000000 // 0 0
563
564// SX1272_REG_PLL_HOP + SX1278_REG_PLL_HOP
565#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FAST_HOP_OFF 0b00000000 // 7 7 carrier frequency validated when FRF registers are written
566#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_FAST_HOP_ON 0b10000000 // 7 7 carrier frequency validated when FS modes are requested
567
568// SX1272_REG_TCXO + SX1278_REG_TCXO
569#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_TCXO_INPUT_EXTERNAL 0b00000000 // 4 4 use external crystal oscillator
570#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_TCXO_INPUT_EXTERNAL_CLIPPED 0b00010000 // 4 4 use external crystal oscillator clipped sine connected to XTA pin
571
572// SX1272_REG_PLL + SX1278_REG_PLL
573#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PLL_BANDWIDTH_75_KHZ 0b00000000 // 7 6 PLL bandwidth: 75 kHz
574#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PLL_BANDWIDTH_150_KHZ 0b01000000 // 7 6 150 kHz
575#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PLL_BANDWIDTH_225_KHZ 0b10000000 // 7 6 225 kHz
576#define RADIOLIB_SX127X_PLL_BANDWIDTH_300_KHZ 0b11000000 // 7 6 300 kHz (default)
577
578/*!
579 \class SX127x
580 \brief Base class for SX127x series. All derived classes for SX127x (e.g. SX1278 or SX1272) inherit from this base class.
581 This class should not be instantiated directly from Arduino sketch, only from its derived classes.
582*/
583class SX127x: public PhysicalLayer {
584 public:
585 // introduce PhysicalLayer overloads
586 using PhysicalLayer::transmit;
587 using PhysicalLayer::receive;
588 using PhysicalLayer::startTransmit;
589 using PhysicalLayer::startReceive;
590 using PhysicalLayer::readData;
591
592 // constructor
593
594 /*!
595 \brief Default constructor. Called internally when creating new LoRa instance.
596 \param mod Instance of Module that will be used to communicate with the %LoRa chip.
597 */
598 explicit SX127x(Module* mod);
599
600 // basic methods
601
602 /*!
603 \brief Initialization method. Will be called with appropriate parameters when calling initialization method from derived class.
604 \param chipVersions Array of possible values in SPI version register. Used to verify the connection and hardware version.
605 \param numVersions Number of possible chip versions.
606 \param syncWord %LoRa sync word.
607 \param preambleLength Length of %LoRa transmission preamble in symbols.
608 \returns \ref status_codes
609 */
610 int16_t begin(const uint8_t* chipVersions, uint8_t numVersions, uint8_t syncWord, uint16_t preambleLength);
611
612 /*!
613 \brief Reset method. Will reset the chip to the default state using RST pin. Should be implemented in derived class since SX1272 and SX1278 implementations differ.
614 */
615 virtual void reset();
616
617 /*!
618 \brief Initialization method for FSK modem. Will be called with appropriate parameters when calling FSK initialization method from derived class.
619 \param chipVersions Array of possible values in SPI version register. Used to verify the connection and hardware version.
620 \param numVersions Number of possible chip versions.
621 \param freqDev Frequency deviation of the FSK transmission in kHz.
622 \param rxBw Receiver bandwidth in kHz.
623 \param preambleLength Length of FSK preamble in bits.
624 \param enableOOK Flag to specify OOK mode. This modulation is similar to FSK.
625 \returns \ref status_codes
626 */
627 int16_t beginFSK(const uint8_t* chipVersions, uint8_t numVersions, float freqDev, float rxBw, uint16_t preambleLength, bool enableOOK);
628
629 /*!
630 \brief Binary transmit method. Will transmit arbitrary binary data up to 255 bytes long using %LoRa or up to 63 bytes using FSK modem.
631 For overloads to transmit Arduino String or C-string, see PhysicalLayer::transmit.
632 \param data Binary data that will be transmitted.
633 \param len Length of binary data to transmit (in bytes).
634 \param addr Node address to transmit the packet to. Only used in FSK mode.
635 \returns \ref status_codes
636 */
637 int16_t transmit(const uint8_t* data, size_t len, uint8_t addr = 0) override;
638
639 /*!
640 \brief Binary receive method. Will attempt to receive arbitrary binary data up to 255 bytes long using %LoRa or up to 63 bytes using FSK modem.
641 For overloads to receive Arduino String, see PhysicalLayer::receive.
642 \param data Pointer to array to save the received binary data.
643 \param len Number of bytes that will be received. Must be known in advance for binary transmissions.
644 \param timeout Reception timeout in milliseconds. If set to 0,
645 timeout period will be calculated automatically based on the radio configuration.
646 \returns \ref status_codes
647 */
648 int16_t receive(uint8_t* data, size_t len, RadioLibTime_t timeout = 0) override;
649
650 /*!
651 \brief Performs scan for valid %LoRa preamble in the current channel.
652 \returns \ref status_codes
653 */
654 int16_t scanChannel() override;
655
656 /*!
657 \brief Performs scan for LoRa transmission in the current channel. Detects both preamble and payload.
658 \param config Ignored. Implemented only for PhysicalLayer compatibility.
659 \returns \ref status_codes
660 */
661 int16_t scanChannel(const ChannelScanConfig_t &config) override;
662
663 /*!
664 \brief Sets the %LoRa module to sleep to save power. %Module will not be able to transmit or receive any data while in sleep mode.
665 %Module will wake up automatically when methods like transmit or receive are called.
666 \returns \ref status_codes
667 */
668 int16_t sleep() override;
669
670 /*!
671 \brief Sets the %LoRa module to standby.
672 \returns \ref status_codes
673 */
674 int16_t standby() override;
675
676 /*!
677 \brief Sets the %LoRa module to standby.
678 \param mode Standby mode to be used. No effect, implemented only for PhysicalLayer compatibility.
679 \returns \ref status_codes
680 */
681 int16_t standby(uint8_t mode) override;
682
683 /*!
684 \brief Enables direct transmission mode on pins DIO1 (clock) and DIO2 (data).
685 While in direct mode, the module will not be able to transmit or receive packets. Can only be activated in FSK mode.
686 \param frf 24-bit raw frequency value to start transmitting at. Required for quick frequency shifts in RTTY.
687 \returns \ref status_codes
688 */
689 int16_t transmitDirect(uint32_t frf = 0) override;
690
691 /*!
692 \brief Enables direct reception mode on pins DIO1 (clock) and DIO2 (data).
693 While in direct mode, the module will not be able to transmit or receive packets. Can only be activated in FSK mode.
694 \returns \ref status_codes
695 */
696 int16_t receiveDirect() override;
697
698 /*!
699 \brief Disables direct mode and enables packet mode, allowing the module to receive packets. Can only be activated in FSK mode.
700 \returns \ref status_codes
701 */
702 int16_t packetMode();
703
704 // interrupt methods
705
706 /*!
707 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when DIO0 activates.
708 \param func Pointer to interrupt service routine.
709 \param dir Signal change direction.
710 */
711 void setDio0Action(void (*func)(void), uint32_t dir);
712
713 /*!
714 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when DIO0 activates.
715 */
716 void clearDio0Action();
717
718 /*!
719 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when DIO1 activates.
720 \param func Pointer to interrupt service routine.
721 \param dir Signal change direction.
722 */
723 void setDio1Action(void (*func)(void), uint32_t dir);
724
725 /*!
726 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when DIO1 activates.
727 */
728 void clearDio1Action();
729
730 /*!
731 \brief Sets interrupt service routine to call when a packet is received.
732 \param func ISR to call.
733 */
734 void setPacketReceivedAction(void (*func)(void)) override;
735
736 /*!
737 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when a packet is received.
738 */
739 void clearPacketReceivedAction() override;
740
741 /*!
742 \brief Sets interrupt service routine to call when a packet is sent.
743 \param func ISR to call.
744 */
745 void setPacketSentAction(void (*func)(void)) override;
746
747 /*!
748 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when a packet is sent.
749 */
750 void clearPacketSentAction() override;
751
752 /*!
753 \brief Sets interrupt service routine to call when a channel scan is finished.
754 \param func ISR to call.
755 */
756 void setChannelScanAction(void (*func)(void)) override;
757
758 /*!
759 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when a channel scan is finished.
760 */
761 void clearChannelScanAction() override;
762
763 /*!
764 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when FIFO is empty.
765 \param func Pointer to interrupt service routine.
766 */
767 void setFifoEmptyAction(void (*func)(void));
768
769 /*!
770 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when FIFO is empty.
771 */
772 void clearFifoEmptyAction();
773
774 /*!
775 \brief Set FIFO threshold level.
776 Be aware that threshold is also set in setFifoFullAction method.
777 setFifoThreshold method must be called AFTER calling setFifoFullAction!
778 \param threshold Threshold level in bytes.
779 */
780 void setFifoThreshold(uint8_t threshold);
781
782 /*!
783 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when FIFO is full.
784 \param func Pointer to interrupt service routine.
785 */
786 void setFifoFullAction(void (*func)(void));
787
788 /*!
789 \brief Clears interrupt service routine to call when FIFO is full.
790 */
791 void clearFifoFullAction();
792
793 /*!
794 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when FIFO is empty.
795 \param data Pointer to the transmission buffer.
796 \param totalLen Total number of bytes to transmit.
797 \param remLen Pointer to a counter holding the number of bytes that have been transmitted so far.
798 \returns True when a complete packet is sent, false if more data is needed.
799 */
800 bool fifoAdd(uint8_t* data, int totalLen, int* remLen);
801
802 /*!
803 \brief Set interrupt service routine function to call when FIFO is sufficiently full to read.
804 \param data Pointer to a buffer that stores the receive data.
805 \param totalLen Total number of bytes to receive.
806 \param rcvLen Pointer to a counter holding the number of bytes that have been received so far.
807 \returns True when a complete packet is received, false if more data is needed.
808 */
809 bool fifoGet(volatile uint8_t* data, int totalLen, volatile int* rcvLen);
810
811 /*!
812 \brief Clean up after transmission is done.
813 \returns \ref status_codes
814 */
815 int16_t finishTransmit() override;
816
817 /*!
818 \brief Interrupt-driven receive method with default parameters.
819 Implemented for compatibility with PhysicalLayer.
820 \returns \ref status_codes
821 */
822 int16_t startReceive() override;
823
824 /*!
825 \brief Reads data that was received after calling startReceive method. When the packet length is not known in advance,
826 getPacketLength method must be called BEFORE calling readData!
827 \param data Pointer to array to save the received binary data.
828 \param len Number of bytes that will be read. When set to 0, the packet length will be retrieved automatically.
829 When more bytes than received are requested, only the number of bytes requested will be returned.
830 \returns \ref status_codes
831 */
832 int16_t readData(uint8_t* data, size_t len) override;
833
834 /*!
835 \brief Clean up after reception is done.
836 \returns \ref status_codes
837 */
838 int16_t finishReceive() override;
839
840 /*!
841 \brief Interrupt-driven channel activity detection method. DIO1 will be activated when LoRa preamble is detected.
842 DIO0 will be activated if there's no preamble detected before timeout.
843 \returns \ref status_codes
844 */
845 int16_t startChannelScan() override;
846
847 /*!
848 \brief Interrupt-driven channel activity detection method. DIO1 will be activated
849 when LoRa preamble is detected, or upon timeout.
850 \param config Ignored. Implemented only for PhysicalLayer compatibility.
851 \returns \ref status_codes
852 */
853 int16_t startChannelScan(const ChannelScanConfig_t &config) override;
854
855 /*!
856 \brief Read the channel scan result.
857 \returns \ref status_codes
858 */
859 int16_t getChannelScanResult() override;
860
861 // configuration methods
862
863 /*!
864 \brief Sets %LoRa sync word. Only available in %LoRa mode.
865 \param syncWord Sync word to be set.
866 \returns \ref status_codes
867 */
868 int16_t setSyncWord(uint8_t syncWord);
869
870 /*!
871 \brief Sets current limit for over current protection at transmitter amplifier. Allowed values range from 45 to 120 mA in 5 mA steps and 120 to 240 mA in 10 mA steps.
872 \param currentLimit Current limit to be set (in mA).
873 \returns \ref status_codes
874 */
875 int16_t setCurrentLimit(uint8_t currentLimit);
876
877 /*!
878 \brief Sets %LoRa or FSK preamble length. Allowed values range from 6 to 65535 in %LoRa mode or 0 to 65535 in FSK mode.
879 \param preambleLength Preamble length to be set (in symbols when in LoRa mode or bits in FSK mode).
880 \returns \ref status_codes
881 */
882 int16_t setPreambleLength(size_t preambleLength) override;
883
884 /*!
885 \brief Invert FSK preamble polarity. The default (non-inverted) is 0x55, the inverted is 0xAA.
886 \param enable Preamble polarity in FSK mode - 0xAA when true, 0x55 when false.
887 \returns \ref status_codes
888 */
889 int16_t invertPreamble(bool enable);
890
891 /*!
892 \brief Gets frequency error of the latest received packet.
893 \param autoCorrect When set to true, frequency will be automatically corrected.
894 \returns Frequency error in Hz.
895 */
896 float getFrequencyError(bool autoCorrect = false);
897
898 /*!
899 \brief Gets current AFC error.
900 \returns Frequency offset from RF in Hz if AFC is enabled and triggered, zero otherwise.
901 */
902 float getAFCError();
903
904 /*!
905 \brief Gets signal-to-noise ratio of the latest received packet. Only available in LoRa mode.
906 \returns Last packet signal-to-noise ratio (SNR).
907 */
908 float getSNR() override;
909
910 /*!
911 \brief Sets FSK frequency deviation from carrier frequency. Allowed values depend on bit rate setting and must be lower than 200 kHz. Only available in FSK mode.
912 \param freqDev Frequency deviation to be set (in kHz).
913 \returns \ref status_codes
914 */
915 int16_t setFrequencyDeviation(float freqDev) override;
916
917 /*!
918 \brief Sets FSK receiver bandwidth. Allowed values range from 2.6 to 250 kHz. Only available in FSK mode.
919 \param rxBw Receiver bandwidth to be set (in kHz).
920 \returns \ref status_codes
921 */
922 int16_t setRxBandwidth(float rxBw);
923
924 /*!
925 \brief Sets FSK automatic frequency correction bandwidth. Allowed values range from 2.6 to 250 kHz. Only available in FSK mode.
926 \param afcBw Receiver AFC bandwidth to be set (in kHz).
927 \returns \ref status_codes
928 */
929 int16_t setAFCBandwidth(float afcBw);
930
931 /*!
932 \brief Enables or disables FSK automatic frequency correction(AFC)
933 \param isEnabled AFC enabled or disabled
934 \return \ref status_codes
935 */
936 int16_t setAFC(bool isEnabled);
937
938 /*!
939 \brief Controls trigger of AFC and AGC
940 \param trigger one from SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_NONE, SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_RSSI_INTERRUPT, SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_PREAMBLE_DETECT, SX127X_RX_TRIGGER_BOTH
941 \return \ref status_codes
942 */
943 int16_t setAFCAGCTrigger(uint8_t trigger);
944
945 /*!
946 \brief Sets FSK sync word. Allowed sync words are up to 8 bytes long and can not contain null bytes. Only available in FSK mode.
947 \param syncWord Sync word array.
948 \param len Sync word length (in bytes).
949 \returns \ref status_codes
950 */
951 int16_t setSyncWord(uint8_t* syncWord, size_t len) override;
952
953 /*!
954 \brief Sets FSK node address. Calling this method will enable address filtering. Only available in FSK mode.
955 \param nodeAddr Node address to be set.
956 \returns \ref status_codes
957 */
958 int16_t setNodeAddress(uint8_t nodeAddr);
959
960 /*!
961 \brief Sets FSK broadcast address. Calling this method will enable address filtering. Only available in FSK mode.
962 \param broadAddr Broadcast address to be set.
963 \returns \ref status_codes
964 */
965 int16_t setBroadcastAddress(uint8_t broadAddr);
966
967 /*!
968 \brief Disables FSK address filtering.
969 \returns \ref status_codes
970 */
971 int16_t disableAddressFiltering();
972
973 /*!
974 \brief Enables/disables OOK modulation instead of FSK.
975 \param enableOOK Enable (true) or disable (false) OOK.
976 \returns \ref status_codes
977 */
978 int16_t setOOK(bool enableOOK);
979
980 /*!
981 \brief Selects the type of threshold in the OOK data slicer.
982 \param type Threshold type: SX127X_OOK_THRESH_PEAK(default), SX127X_OOK_THRESH_FIXED, SX127X_OOK_THRESH_AVERAGE
983 \returns \ref status_codes
984 */
985 int16_t setOokThresholdType(uint8_t type);
986
987 /*!
988 \brief Period of decrement of the RSSI threshold in the OOK demodulator.
989 \param value Use defines RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_DEC_X_X_CHIP
990 \returns \ref status_codes
991 */
992 int16_t setOokPeakThresholdDecrement(uint8_t value);
993
994 /*!
995 \brief Fixed threshold for the Data Slicer in OOK mode or floor threshold for the Data Slicer in OOK when Peak mode is used.
996 \param value Threshold level in steps of 0.5 dB.
997 \returns \ref status_codes
998 */
999 int16_t setOokFixedOrFloorThreshold(uint8_t value);
1000
1001 /*!
1002 \brief Size of each decrement of the RSSI threshold in the OOK demodulator.
1003 \param value Step size: RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_0_5_DB (default), RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_1_0_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_1_5_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_2_0_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_3_0_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_4_0_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_5_0_DB, RADIOLIB_SX127X_OOK_PEAK_THRESH_STEP_6_0_DB
1004 \returns \ref status_codes
1005 */
1006 int16_t setOokPeakThresholdStep(uint8_t value);
1007
1008 /*!
1009 \brief Enable Bit synchronizer.
1010 \returns \ref status_codes
1011 */
1012 int16_t enableBitSync();
1013
1014 /*!
1015 \brief Disable Bit synchronizer (not allowed in Packet mode).
1016 \returns \ref status_codes
1017 */
1018 int16_t disableBitSync();
1019
1020 /*!
1021 \brief Query modem for the packet length of received payload.
1022 \param update Update received packet length. Will return cached value when set to false.
1023 \returns Length of last received packet in bytes.
1024 */
1025 size_t getPacketLength(bool update = true) override;
1026
1027 /*!
1028 \brief Get LoRa header information from last received packet. Only valid in explicit header mode.
1029 \param cr Pointer to variable to store the coding rate.
1030 \param hasCRC Pointer to variable to store the CRC status.
1031 \returns \ref status_codes
1032 */
1033 int16_t getLoRaRxHeaderInfo(uint8_t* cr, bool* hasCRC);
1034
1035 /*!
1036 \brief Set modem in fixed packet length mode. Available in FSK mode only.
1037 \param len Packet length.
1038 \returns \ref status_codes
1039 */
1040 int16_t fixedPacketLengthMode(uint8_t len = RADIOLIB_SX127X_MAX_PACKET_LENGTH_FSK);
1041
1042 /*!
1043 \brief Set modem in variable packet length mode. Available in FSK mode only.
1044 \param maxLen Maximum packet length.
1045 \returns \ref status_codes
1046 */
1047 int16_t variablePacketLengthMode(uint8_t maxLen = RADIOLIB_SX127X_MAX_PACKET_LENGTH_FSK);
1048
1049 /*!
1050 \brief Convert from bytes to LoRa symbols.
1051 \param len Payload length in bytes.
1052 \param dr Data rate.
1053 \param pc Packet configuration.
1054 \returns The total number of LoRa symbols, including preamble, sync and possible header.
1055 */
1056 float getNumSymbols(size_t len, DataRate_t dr, PacketConfig_t pc);
1057
1058 /*!
1059 \brief Get expected time-on-air for a given size of payload.
1060 \param len Payload length in bytes.
1061 \returns Expected time-on-air in microseconds.
1062 */
1063 RadioLibTime_t getTimeOnAir(size_t len) override;
1064
1065 /*!
1066 \brief Calculate the expected time-on-air for a given modem, data rate, packet configuration and payload size.
1067 \param modem Modem type.
1068 \param dr Data rate.
1069 \param pc Packet config.
1070 \param len Payload length in bytes.
1071 \returns Expected time-on-air in microseconds.
1072 */
1073 RadioLibTime_t calculateTimeOnAir(ModemType_t modem, DataRate_t dr, PacketConfig_t pc, size_t len) override;
1074
1075 /*!
1076 \brief Calculate the timeout value for this specific module / series (in number of symbols or units of time)
1077 \param timeoutUs Timeout in microseconds to listen for
1078 \returns Timeout value in a unit that is specific for the used module
1079 */
1080 RadioLibTime_t calculateRxTimeout(RadioLibTime_t timeoutUs) override;
1081
1082 /*!
1083 \brief Read currently active IRQ flags.
1084 \returns IRQ flags.
1085 */
1086 uint32_t getIrqFlags() override;
1087
1088 /*!
1089 \brief Set interrupt on DIO1 to be sent on a specific IRQ bit (e.g. RxTimeout, CadDone).
1090 NOTE: Unlike other modules that support IRQ abstraction (SX126x, LR11x0, etc.),
1091 SX127x cannot configure multiple IRQs to signal using the same DIOx pin.
1092 This method tries to configure IRQs in a "best effort" approach, and will skip conflicting flags.
1093 RADIOLIB_ERR_INVALID_IRQ will be returned in this case.
1094 \param irq Module-specific IRQ flags.
1095 \returns \ref status_codes
1096 */
1097 int16_t setIrqFlags(uint32_t irq) override;
1098
1099 /*!
1100 \brief Clear interrupt on a specific IRQ bit (e.g. RxTimeout, CadDone).
1101 \param irq Module-specific IRQ flags.
1102 \returns \ref status_codes
1103 */
1104 int16_t clearIrqFlags(uint32_t irq) override;
1105
1106 /*!
1107 \brief Enable CRC filtering and generation.
1108 \param enable Set or unset CRC filtering and generation.
1109 \returns \ref status_codes
1110 */
1111 int16_t setCrcFiltering(bool enable = true);
1112
1113 /*!
1114 \brief Sets RSSI measurement configuration in FSK mode.
1115 \param smoothingSamples Number of samples taken to average the RSSI result.
1116 numSamples = 2 ^ (1 + smoothingSamples), allowed values are in range 0 (2 samples) - 7 (256 samples)
1117 \param offset Signed RSSI offset that will be automatically compensated. 1 dB per LSB, defaults to 0, allowed values are in range -16 dB to +15 dB.
1118 \returns \ref status_codes
1119 */
1120 int16_t setRSSIConfig(uint8_t smoothingSamples, int8_t offset = 0);
1121
1122 /*!
1123 \brief Sets transmission encoding. Only available in FSK mode.
1124 Allowed values are RADIOLIB_ENCODING_NRZ, RADIOLIB_ENCODING_MANCHESTER and RADIOLIB_ENCODING_WHITENING.
1125 \param encoding Encoding to be used.
1126 \returns \ref status_codes
1127 */
1128 int16_t setEncoding(uint8_t encoding) override;
1129
1130 /*!
1131 \brief Reads currently active IRQ flags, can be used to check which event caused an interrupt.
1132 In LoRa mode, this is the content of SX127X_REG_IRQ_FLAGS register.
1133 In FSK mode, this is the contents of SX127X_REG_IRQ_FLAGS_2 (MSB) and SX127X_REG_IRQ_FLAGS_1 (LSB) registers.
1134 \returns IRQ flags.
1135 */
1136 uint16_t getIRQFlags();
1137
1138 /*!
1139 \brief Reads modem status. Only available in LoRa mode.
1140 \returns Modem status.
1141 */
1142 uint8_t getModemStatus();
1143
1144 /*!
1145 \brief Reads uncalibrated temperature value. This function will change operating mode
1146 and should not be called during Tx, Rx or CAD.
1147 \returns Uncalibrated temperature sensor reading.
1148 */
1149 int8_t getTempRaw();
1150
1151 /*! \copydoc Module::setRfSwitchPins */
1152 void setRfSwitchPins(uint32_t rxEn, uint32_t txEn);
1153
1154 /*! \copydoc Module::setRfSwitchTable */
1155 void setRfSwitchTable(const uint32_t (&pins)[Module::RFSWITCH_MAX_PINS], const Module::RfSwitchMode_t table[]);
1156
1157 /*!
1158 \brief Get one truly random byte from RSSI noise.
1159 \returns TRNG byte.
1160 */
1161 uint8_t randomByte() override;
1162
1163 /*!
1164 \brief Read version SPI register. Should return SX1278_CHIP_VERSION (0x12) or SX1272_CHIP_VERSION (0x22) if SX127x is connected and working.
1165 \returns Version register contents or \ref status_codes
1166 */
1167 int16_t getChipVersion();
1168
1169 /*!
1170 \brief Enable/disable inversion of the I and Q signals
1171 \param enable IQ inversion enabled (true) or disabled (false);
1172 \returns \ref status_codes
1173 */
1174 int16_t invertIQ(bool enable) override;
1175
1176 /*!
1177 \brief Get modem currently in use by the radio.
1178 \param modem Pointer to a variable to save the retrieved configuration into.
1179 \returns \ref status_codes
1180 */
1181 int16_t getModem(ModemType_t* modem) override;
1182
1183 /*! \copydoc PhysicalLayer::stageMode */
